                                                                        to open the garage door, it may be a BROKEN SPRING. If the door cocks to one side

                                                                        door opener and you may burn it out. Most garage door springs last between 6 to
                                                                        12 years on average. Sometimes garage door springs can last up to 30 years. The
                                                                        more often you use your garage door the less often garage door springs brake. People
                                                                        that use there garages primarily for storage and open there garage doors once a
                                                                        month normally will have garage door springs brake every 2 to 4 years. The average
                                                                        two car garage door is opened 6 to 10 times per day. Garage doors, garage door openers

<b>Broken Garage Door Springs </b>



<p>
GARAGE DOOR SPRINGS for a one piece garage door, or a sectional garage door, on average last 6 to 12 years. BROKEN GARAGE DOOR SPRINGS are caused by a verity of factors. When pouring the steel to make the wire for the springs all air bubbles may not escape causing the garage door spring wire to fault at a later date under pressure. When heat treating the garage door spring wire, the wire as it cools if there is any inconsistence in its cooling can cause a fault under pressure over time. Garage door springs when they break if they&#8217;re older the 5 years of age should all be replaced. Why? Because it is cheaper and more cost effective to replace the other springs then to pay for a second service call within a short period of time of the next spring breaking. Broken Sectional garage door springs on average take between 30 minutes and 90 minutes to replace depending on if there is one spring or two springs if the garage area we work in is clean and easy to more our ladders in. The repair costs of broken sectional garage door springs with labor are between $145.00 to $285.00. Broken one piece garage door springs will range in price including labor $ 105.00 to 275.00 for standard garage door springs. We offer same day service in most cases of garage door spring repair. We cover a large service area.
</p>

<p>
The springs on your garage door can pose a safety hazard. A garage door spring that breaks or shatters can send sharp shrapnel flying in any direction of the garage. Anyone inside the garage if that happens to hit is at serious risk of injury or death. New garage door spring over the last 15 years or so have steel rods inside the center of the garage door spring to help from exploding outward or flying through your roof as well as safety hooks to keep the spring on the hardware. 
</p>

<p>
Modern roll up garage door styles or also known as sectional garage doors pose little risk in the event of spring breakage or shattering. These kinds of springs are installed over a shaft that helps roll the door up to the open position. The shaft also acts as a retainer so that broken springs are not allowed to go ballistic. 
</p>

<p>
If your old garage door springs do not include any such rod, it's best to replace them by call us and schedule an appointment.
</p>

<p>
One piece garage door safety spring sizes. These springs are manufactured by Holmes, King, American and Apex
9 x 28&#8221;, LI 7 x 28&#8221;, standard 7 x 28&#8221;, 5 x 28&#8221;, 3 x 28&#8221;, 1 x 28&#8221; 
</p>

<p>
Residential sectional garage door springs; torsion springs for steel garage doors.
Wire size for metal or steel doors 207, 218, 225, 234, 243. 
</p>

<p>
Residential sectional garage door springs; torsion springs for wood garage doors.
Wire size for wood doors<br />
207, 218, 225, 234, 243, 250, 262, 273.<br />
207 x 26&#8221;, 218 x 26&#8221;, 225 x 26&#8221;, 234 x 32&#8221;, 243 x 35&#8221;, 250 x 36&#8221;, 262 x 36&#8221;, 273 x 42&#8221;<br />
These are standard spring sizes we keep on our trucks.<br />
</p>


<b>Repair Garage Door Opener / Garage Door Operator</b>

<p>
Garage door Chain Drive operators
Need little maintenance just oil the chain drive opener with 20 or 30 weight motor oil once every 3 to 5 years depending on the location of where you live? You can also use WD-40. Have your garage door professional service at least every 5 years. We will check your garage door for balancing, worn parts, we will also lubricate and service the garage door and opener. Most people don&#8217;t realize that garage door springs loose tension over the years and need to be readjusted. If you don&#8217;t keep your garage door well balanced it put extra stress on your garage door opener and reduces its life span. 
</p>


<p>
Screw Drive garage door operators 
Need very little maintenance. Screw drive garage door openers need multi purpose grease on the screw shaft every 2 to 3 years depending on location of where you live and how often you use your garage door operator. You can buy this grease at any hardware or home build store. Have your garage door professional service at least every 5 years. 
</p>

<p>

How do I select the right garage door opener and brand? 
Before selecting an opener, you will need to determine the size and weight of your garage door. This will help to determine the size of the motor needed to lift the garage door. 1/3 HP is more then enough to lift most garage doors. If you have a heavy garage door you should get a Â½ HP. Keep in mind that for very little money difference the Â½ HP garage door openers also gives a better parts warranty. All garage door operators offer most of the same type of safety devices, features and accessories that you want so don&#8217;t get caught up in sales pitches. Your garage door opener is an important home appliance that will get daily use for many years to come. When making this important purchase safety, reliability, horsepower, drive type and quality of installation is important. We have been installing garage door openers for more than 44 years, and can offer you expert advice about selecting and installing your new garage door opener. 
</p>


<p>
Our advice when selecting a garage door opener by brand and model Genie makes a good screw drive garage door opener and has for 50 years in an ( AC motor only) don&#8217;t buy the DC motors these unites they have had some problems in the past. Genie chain drive garage door openers have always stunk in my opinion, Liftmaster makes and always has made a better chain drive garage door opener then Genie. Liftmaster also makes a good screw drive garage door opener as well, but I prefer Genie Â½ HP AC motor over Liftmaster screw drives. Now for the belt drive garage door openers I think they both make a good belt drive you can&#8217;t go wrong either way, but if it was going in my house I would install a Liftmaster belt drive. I hope this information helps you and I hope to earn your business please call us for all your garage door repair or service needs as well as your purchases of a new garage door operators. 
</p>

<p>
What&#8217;s the difference between belt drive, screw drive, chain drive? 
Most make for an effective garage door openers (depending on the brand), but each has its own advantages (depending on the brand). 
</p>

<p>
Belt drive Garage Door Openers - Belt drives are quiet garage door openers at first but 5 to 10 years latter they sound just like most other garage door openers on average. They don&#8217;t use chains, so there is no noise from metal-on-metal contact. But belt drives have bearings that can wear after years of use. Belt-driven garage door openers are a heavy-duty maximum lifting machine with a normally quiet operation. I would buy a Liftmaster garage door opener over a genie garage door opener 
</p>


<p>
Screw drive garage door openers - Screw drives the industry innovations work dog features a solid-steel direct drive for increased strength. Direct drives have unmatched reliability, too. They have no belts, chains or gears to wear out. And their simplistic design &#8212; the motor shaft connects to the drive screw with a coupler &#8212; allows power to be transmitted in a straight line to maximize motor efficiency with minimal loss of torque or power. But screw drives can be less quiet than belt drives at the when first purchased. Both Genie and Liftmaster make good screw drives. Garage door repairs on these models of machines are not very frequent. 
</p>


<p>
Chain Drive Garage Door Openers - Chain Drives are among the most affordable type of garage door operator. They are great on single garage doors both wood and metal, light weight sectional metal garage doors, they are priced a little lower then screw drives or belt drives machines. Chain drive garage door openers just like all the other machine will last a good 15 to 20 years or more as long as your garage door is well balanced. Liftmaster makes the best chain drive on the market Genie never made a very good chain drive unite but keeps trying 
</p>


<p>
Sears or Craftsman garage door openers are made by Liftmaster. All home building store units from Home Depot, Lowe&#8217;s, Orchard, Ace Hardware, Contractors Warehouse, HD supplies, True Value, Sears have a 3 piece track system which is not as strong as the professional garage door openers. Plus when you by a garage door operator from Home Depot, Lowe&#8217;s, Orchard, Ace Hardware, Contractors Warehouse,  HD supplies, True Value, Sears The price is normally higher if you add up all the little charges then if you bough the garage door opener from a professional garage door company here&#8217;s why. Home Depot, Lowe&#8217;s, Orchard, Ace Hardware, Contractors Warehouse,  HD supplies, True Value, Sears charge $159.00 to $220.00 for a garage door opener depending on the horse power and model then you add sales tax sometimes they only come with one remote control so there&#8217;s an other $24.00 to $ 32.00 for the second transmitter. The installation cost between $110.00 to $150.00 and the service contract that cost between $69.00 to $114.00 is sold separately. Then on top of this sear for instance will charge you to balance the garage door if needed or for adjustment to the garage door if needed which will cost you another service call because that&#8217;s another mans job outside of the installer. Any garage door company will balance your garage door service the garage door as part of there installation because they want there machine being installed on a door that&#8217;s not going to be destroying the new garage door opener causing them warranty issues.

Even if you have Home Depot, Lowe&#8217;s, Orchard, Ace Hardware, Contractors Warehouse,  HD supplies, True Value, Sears install the garage door opener for you if you haven&#8217;t purchased a service warranty you normally have 16 days to return your garage door opener if you have problems otherwise you will be referred to the manufacture that&#8217;s when I say good luck!

<b>Garage Door Inspection </b><br />
Garage doors, garage door hardware, garage door springs and garage door openers should be checked for loose, worn or broken parts at least four times a year. You can also inspect your garage door while doing your by-monthly oiling of all the moving parts of your garage door. Oil wheels, hinges, shafts of wheels, and all moving parts with any type of oil, WD40 works well and it&#8217;s easy to use. Keeping your garage door well oiled this will help reduce garage door repairs in the future. Have your garage door professional service at least once every 5 years. <br /><br />
